     <script type="text/javascript">
      $('input[placeholder], textarea[placeholder]').placeholder();    
  /*$('#mn_cogwheel_dropdown ul').append( $('#extra-cp&gt;li').detach() );*/
  /*$('#mbn_after_cog').append( $('#mbn_form_notifications&gt;a').detach() );*/
  $('#sn_s2_min li').hide();
  $('#sn_s2_min li:eq(0)').show();
  $('#sn_s2_min ul').css('display','inline');

  // Animate Trending forums in collapsed view
  $(function() { 
  window.setInterval( function() {
     var n = $('#sn_s2_min li:visible').next();
     if(n.length==0) n = $('#sn_s2_min li:eq(0)');
      
     $('#sn_s2_min li:visible').hide(250,'linear',function() {
       n.show(250);
     });
  }, 5000);
  });

  // Enable toggle between collapse/expand view
  $('#sn_minimize').click( function() {
    $(this).parent().toggleClass('expanded');
    $.cookie('spe_supernav_collapsed',!$(this).parent().hasClass('expanded'),{ expires: 365, path: '/' });
    return false;
  });

  var supernav_state = $.cookie('spe_supernav_collapsed');
  
    if( supernav_state != "false" ) $('#sn_minimize').parent().toggleClass('expanded');
     </script>

                  <div class="postrow has_after_content">
                   <h2 class="title icon">
                    <img alt="Red face" src="http://forums.crackberry.com/images/icons/icon11.png"/>
                    Change "5 Bar" display to signal power dBM
                   </h2>
                   <div class="content">
                    <div id="post_message_210594">
                     <blockquote class="postcontent restore ">
                      Thursday, March 27 2008, @ 6:47 AM (-0800 GMT)
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Hi All,
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      I published this info here several months back, but have since added more to it. The "5 Bar" signal level display, at the top right corner of your 8820 display is, "cute," but of little practical use as it is too vague and insensitive. With a more accurate, and sensitive way to indicate signal power, you can experiment with "how" you physically "hold" and use your BB, try an external antenna in remote locations, keep a "handle" on receiver sensitivity, etc.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      A far better way to indicate cell tower signal strength is to display the actual signal power in "dBM." This is the signal power level, in decibels, referenced to a signal power of 1 milliwatt. The level will ALWAYS be a "negative" number as your signal level will always be less than 1 milliwatt, much less.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      To change your display from "5 Bars" to signal power in dBM, do the following: With one finger, hold down the ALT key on the far left. Now, with your other hand, press the letter sequence NMLL. Your display should instantly change  from "5 Bar" to signal power in dBM. To revert BACK to "5 Bar," do the same thing again.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      There is ONE CAVEAT in doing this. An extremely WEAK signal, less than or equal -100 dBM, will NOT show on-screen becuz only 2 digits can be displayed. So, when your signal level gets VERY VERY weak, at, say, -99 dBM, a further drop will change the display to "-10," then "-11" etc, corresponding to signal powers in the -100 to -119 dBM range. This is of no real problem tho, as your phone probably wont work at that low a level anyway, BUT you can experiment with an iinduction coupled external antenna if you want. Also, it is highly unlikely you will ever see a signal level HIGHER than about -40 dBM, i.e. -39, -38, yada yada, dBM.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      For those who are technically oriented, as most BB Users are, and want MORE, here is an approximate tabulation of the # of Bars vs. signal level in dBM:
                      <br/>
                      1 bar ~ -102 to -120 dBM
                      <br/>
                      2 Bars ~ -93 to -101 dBM
                      <br/>
                      3 Bars ~ -87 to -92 dBM
                      <br/>
                      4 Bars ~ -78 to -86 dBM
                      <br/>
                      5 Bars ~ -40 to -77 dBM
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      I hope this is helpful information? i have learned a LOT from the Crackberry forums and am trying to "payback" in a way that I can.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      If you participate in the 3D Virtual World of SL, "Second Life,"
                      <a href="http://www.secondlife.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                       Second Life: Official site of the 3D online virtual world
                      </a>
                      , visit me "in-world." My name there is Linda Latte. We can "do lunch" on the SS Titanic, back in 1912, before it sinks.  &lt;giggle&gt; YES, it "exists" there, really!  Hahahaha.  If you don't "do" SL, visit my web site for FREE antispam software. Its at
                      <a href="http://www.AntiSpamYellowPages.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                       FREE antispam software. Free spam blockers you can download.
                      </a>
                     </blockquote>
                    </div>
                   </div>

                   <h2 class="title icon">
                    <img alt="Default" src="http://forums.crackberry.com/images/icons/icon1.png"/>
                   </h2>
                   <div class="content">
                    <div id="post_message_212826">
                     <blockquote class="postcontent restore ">
                      <div class="bbcode_container">
                       <div class="bbcode_quote">
                        <div class="quote_container">
                         <div class="bbcode_quote_container">
                         </div>
                         <div class="bbcode_postedby">
                          <img alt="Quote" src="http://forums.crackberry.com/images/misc/quote_icon.png"/>
                          Originally Posted by
                          <strong>
                           linda anne
                          </strong>
                          <a href="http://forums.crackberry.com/tips-how-faq-f3/change-5-bar-display-signal-power-dbm-26381/#post210594" rel="nofollow">
                           <img alt="View Post" class="inlineimg" src="http://forums.crackberry.com/images/buttons/viewpost-right.png"/>
                          </a>
                         </div>
                         <div class="message">
                          For those who are technically oriented, as most BB Users are, and want MORE, here is an approximate tabulation of the # of Bars vs. signal level in dBM:
                          <br/>
                          1 bar ~ -102 to -120 dBM
                          <br/>
                          2 Bars ~ -93 to -101 dBM
                          <br/>
                          3 Bars ~ -87 to -92 dBM
                          <br/>
                          4 Bars ~ -78 to -86 dBM
                          <br/>
                          5 Bars ~ -40 to -77 dBM
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      I live 3 blocks from a cell tower and always have 5 bars on my Pearl but only get -80dBm. I don't think I've ever seen a higher number then that. I didn't use this trick to find out, I just went into Options, Status.
                     </blockquote>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </td>

                      It works for the pearl.  While holding down the ALT button, you need to press the [8/B/N] button twice to get the N before proceeding to press the M, and L buttons
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      ---Edit---
                      <br/>
                      Sorry, need to press the L button twice, so:
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Hold down ALT, press [8/B/N] twice, press M once, press L twice
                      <br/>
                      ---Edit---
                     </blockquote>

          <script type="text/javascript">
           (function($) {

		$.fn.render_mbn_offers = function() {
			$('#mbn-offers-anchor',this).each( function(i,e) {

        $.ajax({
          dataType: "jsonp",
          cache: true,
          jsonpCallback:"mbn_offers_loaded",
          url: $(e).attr('data-href') + "?mode=a&amp;sloc=us,ca,uk",
          data: {},
          success: function(data) {
            $(e).after(data).remove();
          }
        });

			});
			return this;
		};
	})(jQuery);

	$(function(){ $('body').render_mbn_offers();});
          </script>
